  Keep your AI agent configs in sync — automatically.
  Works across Claude Code, Cursor, Codex, and GitHub Copilot.

  How it works:

  1. Connect    Link your LLM provider and select your agents
  2. Setup      Detect stack, install sync hooks & skills
  3. Generate   Audit existing config or generate from scratch
  4. Finalize   Review changes and score your setup

  Step 1/3 — Connect

  Provider: claude-cli | Model: claude-opus-4-7[1m] | Scan: claude-haiku-4-5@20251001

  Target: claude, cursor, github-copilot

  Step 2/4 — Setup

  Installing sync infrastructure...

  ✓ Pre-commit hook — active
  ✓ Onboarding hook — nudges new team members to set up
  ✓ Freshness hook — warns when configs are stale
  ✓ Agent skills installed — /setup-caliber, /find-skills, /save-learning
  ✓ Session learning enabled

  New team members can run /setup-caliber inside their coding agent
  (Claude Code or Cursor) to get set up automatically.

  Current config score:

  88/100 (Grade A)  ·  Claude Code + Cursor + github-copilot  ·  ▓▓▓▓▓▓▓▓▓▓▓▓▓▓▓▓▓▓░░
  ✗ Copilot instructions exist
  ✗ MCP servers configured
  ✗ Learned content present
  ✗ Model & effort pinned
  ✗ External sources configured

  Run /Users/alonpe/.nvm/versions/node/v24.14.0/bin/caliber score for details.
